The revolving restaurant on the top floor of the hotel offers a panoramic view of the Tengwang Pavilion and the scenery on both sides of the Ganjiang River. The buffet breakfast in the revolving restaurant on the top floor of the hotel is a major feature of the hotel. I compared the hotels near the Tengwang Pavilion and finally decided to book this hotel for the breakfast in the revolving restaurant on the top floor.
